   00 | ------ IMark(0x400400, 4, 1) ------
   01 | t2 = GET:I32(lr)
   02 | t4 = Shl32(t2,0x01)
   03 | t5 = Add32(t2,t4)
   04 | ------ IMark(0x400404, 4, 1) ------
   05 | t10 = Shl32(t5,0x03)
   06 | t11 = Add32(t5,t10)
   07 | PUT(pc) = 0x00400409
   08 | ------ IMark(0x400408, 4, 1) ------
   09 | t14 = GET:I32(sp)
   10 | t15 = Add32(t14,0x0000006c)
   11 | STle(t15) = t11
   12 | ------ IMark(0x40040c, 4, 1) ------
